***slobber.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a> (99760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span></span>; ultimately a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slabber</i>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slob</i>, which derives from Irish.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">slobbers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Liquid material, generally saliva, that dribbles or drools outward and downward from the mouth.
<dl><dd><i>There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> dried <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slobber.html>slobber</a></b> on his coat lapel.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Muddy or marshy <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>; mire.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A jellyfish.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sloep.html>sloep</a> (14796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">chaloupe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">chaloppe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nutshell, seed husk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">eschalope</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pod, shell, nutshell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably a blend of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">eschale</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">envelope</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">casing, wrap, covering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***slof.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slof.html>slof</a> (29063)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably form the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sloven.html>sloven</a></i>, which originally meant “to glide, to push”. Compare regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schluffen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slipper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slof.html>slof</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sloffen.html>sloffen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slof.html>slofje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>house or bedroom slipper <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">shoe</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:slof.html>slof</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sloop.html>sloop</a> (8147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slope</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slōpa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slaupǭ</i>.
</p>

***sloppenwijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sloppenwijk.html>sloppenwijk</a> (34681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slop.html>slop</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alleyway, narrow passage between <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neighborhood, district</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***slordig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slordig.html>slordig</a> (7435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">slodderen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to muddle up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schluderig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">botched, slipshod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. 
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>sloppy, careless</li>
<li>undisciplined, haphazard</li>
<li>unkempt, untidy, slovenly</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slutą</i>.

***sluis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sluis.html>sluis</a> (19998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sluse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">slūsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exclūsa</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sclūsa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sluice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exclūsus</i>, form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">exclūdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I shut out, I exclude</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sluice</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluis.html>sluis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluizen.html>sluizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluis.html>sluisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sluice, lock</li></ol>

<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

***sluiten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a> (1194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sluten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slūtan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slūtaną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sleutaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lock, shut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to close</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make, to affirm <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a pact, friendship etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijanden.html>vijanden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriendschap.html>vriendschap</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesloten.html>gesloten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The two enemies <b>made</b> friends.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verschilden.html>verschilden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mening.html>mening</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:compromis.html>compromis</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gesloten.html>gesloten</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They differed in opinion, but they still <b>made</b> a compromise.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slutere</i>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slurven.html>slurven</a></i> (a variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slurpen.html>slurpen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:slurp.html>slurp</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slorf</i>.

***slurp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slurp.html>slurp</a> (62974)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A variant form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slurf.html>slurf</a></i> which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> instead directly derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slurpen.html>slurpen</a></i>; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slurf.html>slurf</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived through the variant form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slurven.html>slurven</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***slush.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a> (79547)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Most likely imitative; related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">slosh</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">slushes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Half-melted snow or ice.
<dl><dd><i>As the skiing season <a href = vnd.unilang:drew.html>drew</a> to an end, there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> nothing but <b><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a></b> left on the <a href = vnd.unilang:piste.html>piste</a>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Liquid mud or mire.</li>
<li>Flavored shaved ice served as a <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>.</li>
<li>A soft mixture of grease and other materials, used for lubrication.</li>
<li>The refuse grease and fat collected in cooking, especially on shipboard.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mixture of white lead and lime, used as a paint to prevent oxidation.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">publishing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Unsolicited manuscripts, as in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a> pile</i>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">snow</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a> ice</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">flavored shaved ice served as a <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">slushy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">slushie</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">slurpee</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Slurpee</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a> puppy</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>Slush</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:puppie.html>Puppie</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slush.html>slush</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">slushes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">slushing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">slushed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To smear with slushy liquid or grease.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b> July 9,  Donald G. Mcneil,  “Restless <a href = vnd.unilang:pioneers.html>Pioneers</a>, Seeding Brooklyn”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/07/09/dining/09brook.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The ungrateful “they” are Brooklynites who’ve come to see Harding-Mamary creations as a chain, where you can get it <a href = vnd.unilang:venti.html>venti</a> in a ramekin with crème fraîche or <b>slushed</b> with guava and salt on the rim.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To slosh or splash; to move as, or through, a slushy or liquid substance.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1902</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>Jack</a> London,  <cite>The Cruise of the Dazzler</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/11051">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The water <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> soon <b>slushing</b> merrily <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the deck, while the smoke pouring from the cabin stove carried a promise of good <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> to come.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1994</b> March 4,  <a href = vnd.unilang:dave.html>Dave</a> Wiethop, Sandi Abadinski,  “Reader to Reader”, in  <cite>Chicago Reader</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://securesite.chireader.com/cgi-bin/Archive/abridged2.bat?path=1994/940304/RTR">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Sitting inside the Starbucks on <a href = vnd.unilang:broadway.html>Broadway</a> near <a href = vnd.unilang:roscoe.html>Roscoe</a>, two art students <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> tired of sketching people <b>slushing</b> through the two-day-old snow.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1919</b>,  F. Scott Fitzgerald,  <cite>This Side of Paradise</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/805">[4]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A belated freshman, his oilskin slicker rasping loudly, <b>slushed</b> along the soft path.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1918</b>,  Randall Parrish,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:wolves.html>Wolves</a> of the Sea</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/10210">[5]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The deck below <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> littered with chests, sea boots, and <a href = vnd.unilang:odds.html>odds</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> of clothing, while farther aft considerable water <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> found entrance through the scuttle hole, and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b>slushing</b> back and forth as the bark rolled.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1907</b>,  Nicholas <a href = vnd.unilang:carter.html>Carter</a>,  <cite>A Woman at Bay</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/26704">[6]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">They climbed <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> fallen and moss-grown <a href = vnd.unilang:logs.html>logs</a>; they <b>slushed</b> through shallow water; they crawled on their hands and knees under embankments and rocks, and at last, at Handsome's order, they stepped into a boat of some <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> which the latter <a href = vnd.unilang:pushed.html>pushed</a> away from the bank with a pole.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1888</b>,  Wilfrid Chateauclair,  <cite>The Young <a href = vnd.unilang:seigneur.html>Seigneur</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/15256">[7]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But as the boat stuck in the bottom and refused to stir, he suddenly dropped his hold, and with an "<a href = vnd.unilang:avance.html>Avance</a> done!" gallantly <b>slushed</b> his way into the water alongside, in his Sunday trousers, lifted the gunwale and started her afloat, amidst a shower of final "<a href = vnd.unilang:au.html>Au</a> revoirs," and the <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> <i>chaloupe</i> moved with noiseless smoothness down the current.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1867</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:frank.html>Frank</a> Jardine and Alexander Jardine,  <cite>The Overland Expedition of The Messrs. Jardine</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/etext/4521">[8]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The creek at last crossed, the party attempted to push forward on the other side, but after travelling a mile leading the <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a>, <b>slushing</b> through bog and swamp under a heavy rain, they <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> obliged to turn back and encamp on some high ground on the <a href = vnd.unilang:banks.html>banks</a> of the creek, about half-a-mile above the crossing, where there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a little good grass.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To paint with a mixture of white lead and lime.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">smade</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smēhijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to despise, belittle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*smēyg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small, thin, delicate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">smá</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scorn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smikraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fine, fair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:smachten.html>smachten</a></i>, ultimately from a variant of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*smēhaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">small, little</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μικρός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mikrós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a little of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mica.html>mica</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:smak.html>smak</a> (15248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">smacken</i>, of imitative origin. See also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schmatzen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smack</i>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">smash</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smak.html>smak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smakken.html>smakken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:smak.html>smakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>crash, blow, smack</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
